---
title     : "TypedBarendregt: Raw terms with types (broken)"
layout    : page
permalink : /TypedBarendregt
---

This version uses raw terms. Substitution presumes that no
generation of fresh names is required.

The substitution algorithm is based on one by McBride.
It is given a map from names to terms. Say the mapping of a
name is trivial if it takes a name to a term consisting of
just the variable with that name. No fresh names are required
if the mapping on each variable is either trivial or to a
closed term. However, the proof of correctness currently
contains a hole, and may be difficult to repair.

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Val-⟶"></a><a id="12931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12937" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12939" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12941" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12942" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12945" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12947" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9176" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="12955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12942" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12957" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12959" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="12961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12942" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9443" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12944" class="Bound">N</a><a id="12967" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12969" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9326" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="12979" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="12982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="12988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9204" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="12993" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="12996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9249" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="13007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13007" class="Bound">VM</a><a id="13009" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9758" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="13018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13018" class="Bound">M⟶N</a><a id="13021" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="13024" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13027" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13007" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13018" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟶-Val"></a><a id="13115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13115" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13121" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13123" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13125" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13126" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13128" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13128" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13129" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13133" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13134" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13126" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13136" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9443" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13128" class="Bound">N</a><a id="13139" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13141" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13143" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="13145" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9176" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="13151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13126" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="13153" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13115" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="13159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13159" class="Bound">M⟶N</a> <a id="13163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13163" class="Bound">VM</a>  <a id="13167" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="13170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#12931" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13163" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="13179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13159" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Reduction is deterministic

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="det"></a><a id="13239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13239" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13243" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13245" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="13247" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13248" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13250" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="13253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13253" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="13255" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13259" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13261" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13262" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13248" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="13264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#9443" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="13266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13250" class="Bound">M′</a><a id="13268" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="14761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#13239" class="Function">det</a> <a id="14765" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14766" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10519" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14770" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14774" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14776" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#10519" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="14781" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="14785" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14787" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Almost half the lines in the above proof are redundant, for example

    det (ξ-·₁ L⟶L′) (ξ-·₂ VL _) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L′)
    det (ξ-·₂ VL _) (ξ-·₁ L⟶L″) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L″)
 
are essentially identical. What we might like to do is delete the
redundant lines and add

    det M⟶M′ M⟶M″ = sym (det M⟶M″ M⟶M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work. The termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.

## Canonical forms

## Progress

## Preservation

### Domain of an environment

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17873" class="Comment">{-
dom : Ctx → List Id
dom ε            =  []
dom (Γ , x `: A)  =  x ∷ dom Γ

dom-lemma : ∀ {Γ y B} → Γ ∋ y `: B → y ∈ dom Γ
dom-lemma Z           =  here
dom-lemma (S x≢y ⊢y)  =  there (dom-lemma ⊢y)

free-lemma : ∀ {Γ M A} → Γ ⊢ M `: A → free M ⊆ dom Γ
free-lemma (Ax ⊢x) w∈ with w∈
...                      | here         =  dom-lemma ⊢x
...                      | there ()   
free-lemma {Γ} (⊢λ {N = N} ⊢N)          =  ∷-to-\\ (free-lemma ⊢N)
free-lemma (⊢L · ⊢M) w∈ with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...                        | inj₁ ∈L    = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...                        | inj₂ ∈M    = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
free-lemma ⊢zero ()
free-lemma (⊢suc ⊢M) w∈                 = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢pred ⊢M) w∈                = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢if0 ⊢L ⊢M ⊢N) w∈
        with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...         | inj₁ ∈L                   = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...         | inj₂ ∈MN with ++-to-⊎ ∈MN
...                       | inj₁ ∈M     = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
...                       | inj₂ ∈N     = free-lemma ⊢N ∈N
free-lemma (⊢Y ⊢M) w∈                   = free-lemma ⊢M w∈       
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Substitution preserves types

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21703" class="Comment">{-
⊢subst : ∀ {Γ Δ ρ}
  → (∀ {x A} → Δ ∋ x `: A  →  Γ ∋ x `: A)
  → (∀ {x A} → Γ ∋ x `: A  →  Δ ⊢ ρ x `: A)
    --------------------------------------------------------------
  → (∀ {M A} → (⊢M : Γ ⊢ M `: A) →  ok ⊢M  →  Δ ⊢ subst ρ M `: A)
-}</a>
<a id="⊢subst"></a><a id="21947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21947" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="21954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21956" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="21958" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="21959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21959" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="21961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21961" class="Bound">Δ</a> <a id="21963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21963" class="Bound">ρ</a><a id="21964" class="Symbol">}</a>

<a id="23099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21947" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23106" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3025" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23113" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23115" class="Symbol">)</a>                <a id="23132" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="23135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#3025" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="23138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#21947" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="23146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23106" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="23149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23113" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="23151" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let's look at examples.  Assume `M` is closed.  Example 1.

    subst (tm-∅ , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x")  ≡  `λ "y" `→ M

Example 2.

      subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ subst (tm-∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M , "y" ↦ ` "y") (` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ (M · ` "y")

The hypotheses of the theorem appear to be violated. Drat!

  <a id="23599" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23584" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="23603" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#1756" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="23605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23586" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#1756" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`:</a> <a id="23610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23588" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2309" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="23614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23590" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="23616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#2309" class="Datatype Operator">`:</a> <a id="23619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/TypedBarendregt.md %}{% raw %}#23592" class="Bound">B</a>
